 March 18 is the birthday of the evergreen hero Shashi Kapoor
 shashi kapur apni khaas muskaan ke liye bhi jane jate the isi kaa ek andaaj dekhne ke liye film 'jab jab phool khile' kaa gaanaa 'ek tha gul or ek thi bulbul' main unka muskuraataa cheharaa hi kaaphi he
 Let's know some special things related to them
 1
 Shashi Kapoor, born on March 18, 1938, is the youngest of Prithviraj's four children, being called the father of Hindi cinema
 unki maa kaa naam ramsharani kapur tha
 2
 aakarshak vyaktitv vaale shashi kapur ke bachapan kaa naam balbir raaj kapur tha
 a fond of acting since childhood, Shashi wanted to participate in plays in school
 unki yah ichha vahaan to kabhi puri nahin hui, lekin unhen yah mauka apane pita ke 'prithvi theatres' main mila
 3
 shashi ne acting main apana kariyar 1944 main apane pita prithviraj kapur keprithvi theatreke naatak 'shakuntla' se shuru kiya
 He also made his acting debut in films as a child artist
 4
 Even in the case of marriage, he left separately
 prithvi theatre main kaam karne ke dauraan vah bharat yatra par aae godafre candal ke theatre group 'shakesperana' main shaamil ho gaye
 Working with the theater group, he traveled around the world and appeared in several plays with Godfrey's daughter Jennifer
 isi bich unka orjenifer kaa pyaraparavaan chadha or 20 saal kii umr main hi unhone khud se teen saal badi jenifer se shaadi kar lee
 This was the first such marriage in the Kapoor family
 5
 Made films like Junoon, Kalyug, 36 Chowringhee Lane, Utsav under the direction of the legendary filmmakers of the country like Shyam Benegal, Aparna Sen, Govind Nihalani, Girish Karnad
 ye filmein box offis par to safal nahin huin, lekin inhen aalochakon ne kaaphi saraahaa or ye filmein aaj bhi mile kaa pathar maani jaati hai
 6
 shashi kapur bharat ke pehle aise actors main se ek hai, jinhone antarrashtriya str par british or america filmon main bhi kaam kiya
 These include films such as Householder, Shakespeare Walla, Bombay Talkies, and Heat and Dust
 7
 He was also awarded the Dada Saheb Phalkepurskar, for his contribution to Hindi cinema
 8
 He received the National Award as Producer for his film 'junoon', was awarded the National Award for Acting in 'new Delhi Times' and in 2011 he received the Padma Bhushan
 9
 Apart from this, Shashi Kapoor also received the Best Actor for the film Jab Jab Phool Khile, the Bombay Journalist Association Award and the National Award for Special Jury for the film 'muhafiz'
 10
 He is almost retired from Bollywood
 varsh 1998 main ifilm 'jinna'unke sine kariyar kii aakhri film maani ja rahi he
